- `agent.dx_agents.cli_path` now defaults to the root `dx` executable, and Zed GPUI actions use that configured path for the public `dx agents ... --json` bridge instead of hardcoding `dx` while displaying a separate `dx-agents` setting.
- Failed DX Agents GPUI bridge actions now write a redacted `action-error-latest.json` receipt and surface the last failure in Agent Configuration plus the DX launch rail, so missing CLI/path/runtime launch failures are visible without exposing raw stderr secrets.
- DX Agents action-error receipts now carry parsed redaction posture into Agent Configuration and the DX launch rail, warning if a stale or malformed action-error packet claims to export secrets, provider credentials, or receipt bodies.
- DX Agents receipt rows now carry social connected/needs-auth and automation enabled/warning counters from the runtime-owned receipt index into the launch rail without reading run receipt bodies.
- DX Agents connected account summaries now prefer the runtime `needs_auth` field and fall back to `needs_connection`, keeping older receipts readable while making auth-needed state explicit in the Social Accounts rail.
- DX Agents task-state hardening landed in the runtime/CLI receipt contracts: unknown non-redacted run `task_state` values now surface as unsafe or malformed metadata, which the existing Agent receipt rail renders through its review warning path.
- DX Agents contract-audit receipts are now classified by the runtime and CLI receipt indexes, letting the Agent receipt rail distinguish bridge audit evidence from generic cached metadata rows.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio.rs` now treats `.dx/` and `public/preview-manifest.json` as strong DX-WWW project signals and reads object-shaped route maps in addition to route arrays.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio.rs` and the Web Preview page diagnostics now include `data-dx-style-surface` in the DX Studio marker set for dx-style surface inspection.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_session.rs` now exposes manifest index counts for source selection, editable surfaces, edit operations, readiness, and Forge receipts so route/source/package surfaces are inspectable from Web Preview session JSON.
- `crates/web_preview/src/windows_visual_webview.rs` now installs the DX Studio bridge after the existing Web Preview bridge without changing generic Web Preview behavior.
- `crates/web_preview/src/web_preview_view.rs` now stores DX Studio selection/edit receipts, exposes them in session snapshots, adds More-menu actions for selecting DX Studio surfaces and editing DX Studio text, handles WebView IPC edit requests, and forwards source-edit receipts back to the overlay for hot-reload/refresh status.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_bridge.rs` now also exposes a general Edit DX Studio Surface action, captures `data-dx-source-file`, insert slot, reorder group, design token, token scope, media slot, class tokens, and responsive class tokens, and captures a pre-write hot-reload version baseline before requesting a source mutation.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_bridge.rs` now separates detected read-only responsive tokens from editable responsive props, and only marks responsive class tokens editable when the selected surface declares `update_design_token`.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_bridge.rs` now renders structured source-edit refusal status from receipts, so template-required/stale/ambiguous/readonly/generated/runtime failures are visible in the overlay instead of a generic failure label.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit.rs` now acts as a small facade over focused source-edit modules while preserving the existing Web Preview IPC/source-edit behavior.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit.rs` now includes marker requirements, source-template readiness, and structured refusal classification in source-edit plans/receipts.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit.rs` now enriches selected DOM surfaces with JSON-manifest or TypeScript-contract declared source files, materialized files, operation IDs, package IDs, edit-contract summaries, and operation contract metadata before computing source-edit readiness or applying writes.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit.rs` now includes manifest ambiguity metadata in source-edit plans and refuses writes when multiple JSON/TypeScript contract surfaces match the selected DOM marker with equal strength.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit.rs` now includes source file length/modified-time snapshots in source-edit plans and refuses writes when the owning file changes after selection.
- `crates/web_preview/src/web_preview_view.rs` now attaches the current source-edit plan to failed DX Studio edit receipts before sending them back to the WebView overlay.
- `crates/web_preview/src/web_preview_view.rs` now injects the latest matching selection's source freshness snapshot into edit requests so stale token/reorder writes can be refused before file mutation.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit/operations.rs` now keeps operation readiness/routing separate from text, token, reorder, insert, and safety helper implementations, avoiding a single large transformer file.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit/operations/token.rs` now treats responsive class token changes as responsive layout edits and refuses breakpoint-prefix changes such as `md:` to `lg:` so Zed does not rewrite layout across breakpoints.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit.rs` now implements guarded `update_design_token` token/class replacement and `move_reorder_section` group moves against source-owned files through the split operation modules, while keeping `insert_component` and `insert_icon_media` gated on manifest-declared source snippets/templates.
- `crates/web_preview/src/dx_studio_source_edit/operations.rs` and `operations/insert.rs` now treat manifest-carried source snippets/templates as real insert/media readiness, while still refusing insert/media writes when the matched DX-WWW contract does not provide a safe template.
- `crates/web_preview/src/web_preview_view.rs` now exposes the Edit DX Studio Surface action in the Web Preview More menu and session capability metadata.

NOTES:
- Real write support now covers direct source-literal `update_text_content`, source-token/class-token `update_design_token`, and source-range `move_reorder_section` within declared reorder groups. Insert component and icon/media writes are wired but refuse unless a manifest provides a safe source snippet/template.
- Responsive layout edits are intentionally modeled as declared `update_design_token` class-token edits until DX-WWW adds a separate operation; Zed now preserves breakpoint prefixes and reports read-only responsive tokens separately from editable props.
- Insert/media operations remain real contract plumbing but still refuse writes without a manifest source snippet/template; the refusal receipt now says that explicitly and carries the source-edit plan for review.
- Source freshness is guarded by best-effort metadata snapshots from the latest matching selection; if the owning file changes before the edit request reaches Rust, Zed refuses instead of writing stale source.
- DX-WWW inspection showed the generated `examples/conversion-proof/public/preview-manifest.json` and source `examples/launch-template/dx-studio-edit-contract.ts` carry the real `dx.studio.launch_edit_contract.v1` surface and operation contract, but current insert/media operations still do not publish snippets/templates, so Zed keeps those writes refused instead of fabricating UI.
- Verification run: `rustfmt --edition 2024`, `rustfmt --edition 2024 --check`, targeted `git diff --check`, targeted conflict-marker search, ASCII scan on new bridge/edit files, and a Node parse check of the injected DX Studio bridge script.
- No Cargo commands, local servers, browser/WebView runtime testing, DX-WWW CLI execution, or `just run` were executed.

- Managed Chrome `set_viewport` receipts now include requested and applied viewport metadata, including device scale factor evidence.
- Managed Chrome `wait_for_selector` receipts now include selector, requested state, timeout, matched flag, and matched element bounds.
- Agent and WebPreview managed Chrome execution summaries now expose compact `viewport_change` and `selector_wait` receipt summaries.

CHANGED:
- Agent/WebPreview managed Chrome catalogs now advertise `chrome.page.set_viewport` and `chrome.page.wait_for_selector` as receipt-backed safe actions.
- Managed Chrome screenshot receipts now truthfully mark page-script evaluation when receipt metadata reads page dimensions.

NOTES:
- This does not enable click, type, key, scroll, or OS-wide control in managed Chrome. It still requires managed roots, a ready runner receipt, explicit adapter invocation authorization, managed browser profiles, and final Windows runtime proof before runtime-green reporting.

[2026-05-14] - Icon SVG Rendering And Remote Media Fetch

ADDED:
- `crates/icon_picker/src/icon_representative_bodies.tsv` now embeds representative SVG bodies for hardcoded external icon packs so the default All sets grid can warm real previews without opening every source Iconify JSON file.
- `crates/icon_picker` now warms visible external Iconify SVG previews on a background task and caches the generated SVG files before repainting them into the grid.
- `crates/icon_picker` now indexes Iconify aliases in addition to base icons so alternate icon names from each pack appear in panel search and selected-pack grids.
- `crates/editor` now resolves Iconify aliases when inserting dragged or selected external icons, so alias entries create real SVG assets instead of empty files.
- `crates/icon_picker` and `crates/editor` now apply Iconify alias hFlip, vFlip, and rotate metadata when generating previews or inserted SVG assets.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now writes the initial shadcn rkyv catalog cache on a background task when the cache is missing, keeping first panel construction responsive.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches live no-key remote media rows from Openverse, Wikimedia Commons, NASA, Library of Congress, and Art Institute of Chicago for the active media query/filter.
- `crates/media_panel` now uses shared Zed HTTP client plumbing plus JSON parsing for direct provider results instead of relying only on static sample rows.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches remote media results per active query and media tab so repeated searches and tab switches can repaint immediately.
- `crates/media_panel` now debounces remote provider searches and guards them by generation, preventing stale or partial keystroke searches from repainting the panel.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now reuses available local shadcn screenshot assets as panel row thumbnails, with a small in-memory lookup cache.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches The Met public-domain image results directly through its no-key collection API.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches direct NASA video and audio assets by resolving NASA collection manifests into playable media files.
- `crates/media_panel` generated remote-browser pages now search Art Institute and The Met no-key APIs and resolve NASA audio/video manifests to playable files.
- `crates/media_panel` remote media rows now carry optional thumbnail URLs so provider preview images can render in native image, video, and audio rows.
- `crates/media_panel` now runs no-key provider fetches concurrently for first-time remote searches while keeping provider-specific error reporting.
- `crates/media_panel` now overlays compact Zed-themed video/audio badges on remote provider thumbnails so playable media does not read as a plain image row.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches direct Internet Archive image, video, and audio rows by combining no-key advanced search with item metadata/download URLs.
- `crates/media_panel` now caps each remote provider fetch at four seconds so one slow public API cannot block the whole remote media result batch.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches direct Cleveland Museum of Art CC0 image rows through the no-key open access API.

CHANGED:
- `crates/icon_picker` now caps the in-memory external SVG preview cache to the 4096 most recent icon entries while continuing to rely on the on-disk SVG cache for durable preview reuse.
- `crates/icon_picker` now caps warmed external-icon preview batch signatures to the 128 most recent batches, preventing long icon browsing sessions from accumulating stale warm-signature state.
- `crates/media_panel` now caps cached remote media result sets to the 24 most recent query/filter signatures and pre-sizes the cache containers.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches up to 640 remote provider assets per query while keeping the native panel's visible row cap at 320, giving broader provider coverage without increasing the rendered row window.
- `crates/media_panel` now reuses the active remote-results buffer on cache hits and preallocates remote provider, dedupe, and error buffers for remote media fetches.
- `crates/icon_picker` now keeps selected-pack icon loads scoped to `external_icons_by_pack` instead of extending, sorting, and deduping the broad all-icons list on each individual pack open.
- `crates/icon_picker` now preallocates full external Iconify catalog vectors, pack maps, representative rows, per-pack rows, and SVG body maps from known pack sizes, reducing allocator churn during broad icon search and preview generation.
- `crates/icon_picker`, `crates/font_panel`, `crates/media_panel`, and `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now preallocate bounded visible result buffers before collecting search/filter rows, reducing small allocation churn while typing or switching tabs.
- `crates/icon_picker` now caches built-in Zed icon search text so typed searches do not rebuild `DraggedIconAsset` labels for every Zed icon on each repaint.
- `crates/font_panel` now checks cached lowercase font search text in place instead of cloning the cached `SharedString` for every typed-search font match.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now checks cached catalog search text in place instead of cloning the cached `SharedString` for every typed-search row match.
- `crates/icon_picker` now filters cached or already-warming visible external icons before cloning them for preview warm queues.
- `crates/font_panel` now caches lowercase font search text and only builds visible `FontEntry` rows after a font matches a typed query.
- `crates/media_panel` now matches remote media query terms directly against asset fields instead of formatting and lowercasing a combined searchable string for every remote row.
- `crates/icon_picker` now batches external preview-cache checks with one preview-cache borrow and skips icons that are already warming before queuing another SVG preview batch.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now consumes per-render cached thumbnail URLs when building visible rows, avoiding another thumbnail URL clone per row.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now snapshots visible shadcn preview-image cache hits once per render and passes them into row rendering instead of locking the global thumbnail cache for every visible row.
- `crates/icon_picker` now skips render-path preview-file checks for external icons that are already queued for background SVG preview warming.
- `crates/icon_picker` now limits the empty All Sets representative icon collection to the visible result window instead of extending the full external representative catalog and truncating it afterward.
- `crates/icon_picker`, `crates/font_panel`, `crates/media_panel`, and `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now consume the already-filtered visible row vectors when rendering tiles/rows instead of cloning each visible item again.
